# <a name="search-the-audit-log-in-the-security--compliance-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-103">在安全性 & 規範中心搜尋稽核記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-103">Search the audit log in the Security & Compliance Center</span></span>

## <a name="introduction"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-104">簡介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-104">Introduction</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-105">要尋找是否使用者檢視特定的文件，或清除其信箱中的項目？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-105">Need to find if a user viewed a specific document or purged an item from their mailbox?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-106">如果這樣，您可以使用 Office 365 安全性&amp;若要檢視 Office 365 組織中的使用者和系統管理員活動整合的稽核記錄中搜尋的合規性中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-106">If so, you can use the Office 365 Security &amp; Compliance Center to search the unified audit log to view user and administrator activity in your Office 365 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-107">為什麼使用整合的稽核記錄？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-107">Why a unified audit log?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-108">因為您可以搜尋下列類型的 Office 365 中的使用者和系統管理員活動：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-108">Because you can search for the following types of user and admin activity in Office 365:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-109">在 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的使用者活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-109">User activity in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-110">Exchange Online 中的使用者活動 （Exchange 信箱稽核記錄）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-110">User activity in Exchange Online (Exchange mailbox audit logging)</span></span>
    
    > [!IMPORTANT]
    > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-111">信箱稽核記錄必須開啟每個使用者信箱將會記錄在 Exchange Online 中的使用者活動之前。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-111">Mailbox audit logging must be turned on for each user mailbox before user activity in Exchange Online will be logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-112">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 <<c0>啟用 Office 365 中的稽核的信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-112">For more information, see [Enable mailbox auditing in Office 365](enable-mailbox-auditing.md).</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-113">在 SharePoint Online 中的系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-113">Admin activity in SharePoint Online</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-114">在 Azure Active Directory （Office 365 的目錄服務） 的系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-114">Admin activity in Azure Active Directory (the directory service for Office 365)</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-115">Exchange Online 中的系統管理員活動 （Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-115">Admin activity in Exchange Online (Exchange admin audit logging)</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-116">在 Sway 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-116">User and admin activity in Sway</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-117">在安全性與合規性中心的 eDiscovery 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-117">eDiscovery activities in the security and compliance center</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-118">Power BI 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-118">User and admin activity in Power BI</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-119">Microsoft Teams 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-119">User and admin activity in Microsoft Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-120">在 Dynamics 365 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-120">User and admin activity in Dynamics 365</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-121">Yammer 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-121">User and admin activity in Yammer</span></span>
 
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-122">Microsoft Flow 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-122">User and admin activity in Microsoft Flow</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-123">Microsoft Stream 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-123">User and admin activity in Microsoft Stream</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-124">在 Microsoft 工作場所分析中的分析師和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-124">Analyst and admin activity in Microsoft Workplace Analytics</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-125">Microsoft PowerApps 中的使用者和系統管理員活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-125">User and admin activity in Microsoft PowerApps</span></span>
    
   
## <a name="before-you-begin"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-126">開始之前</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-126">Before you begin</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-127">請務必先閱讀下列項目之前開始搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-127">Be sure to read the following items before you start searching the Office 365 audit log.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-128">您 （或另一個系統管理員） 必須先開啟稽核記錄，才能開始搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-128">You (or another admin) must first turn on audit logging before you can start searching the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-129">若要將它開啟，只要按一下 [**開始錄製使用者和系統管理員活動**安全性 & 合規性中心中的**稽核記錄搜尋**] 頁面上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-129">To turn it on, just click **Start recording user and admin activity** on the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-130">（如果您沒有看到此連結，稽核已開啟為您的組織。）您開啟之後，會顯示訊息，指出準備稽核記錄檔以及您可以在幾個小時後準備已完成執行搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-130">(If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.) After you turn it on, a message is displayed that says the audit log is being prepared and that you can run a search in a couple of hours after the preparation is complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-131">您只需要執行這項操作一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-131">You only have to do this once.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-132">我們正在開啟依預設稽核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-132">We're in the process of turning on auditing by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-133">在那之前，您可以將其開啟為先前所述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-133">Until then, you can turn it on as previously described.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-134">您必須獲指派 「 僅檢視稽核記錄檔] 或 [稽核記錄檔角色在 Exchange Online 來搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-134">You have to be assigned the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role in Exchange Online to search the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-135">根據預設，這些角色被指派給在 Exchange 系統管理中心中的**權限**] 頁面上相符性管理] 和 [組織管理角色群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-135">By default, these roles are assigned to the Compliance Management and Organization Management role groups on the **Permissions** page in the Exchange admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-136">請注意，在 Office 365 和 Microsoft 365 的全域系統管理員會自動新增為 Organization Management 角色群組的成員在 Exchange Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-136">Note that global administrators in Office 365 and Microsoft 365 are automatically added as members of the Organization Management role group in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-137">若要讓使用者能夠搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄的最低權限，您可以自訂角色群組 Exchange Online 中建立、 新增 「 僅檢視稽核記錄檔] 或 [稽核記錄 」 角色，並再將使用者新增為新的角色群組的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-137">To give a user the ability to search the Office 365 audit log with the minimum level of privileges, you can create a custom role group in Exchange Online, add the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role, and then add the user as a member of the new role group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-138">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[管理角色群組在 Exchange Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-138">For more information, see [Manage role groups in Exchange Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688).</span></span>
    
    > [!IMPORTANT]
    > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-139">如果您在安全性 & 合規性中心中的 [**權限**] 頁面上的僅檢視稽核記錄檔] 或 [稽核記錄檔角色指派使用者，他們將無法搜尋 Office 365 稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-139">If you assign a user the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role on the **Permissions** page in the Security & Compliance Center, they won't be able to search the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-140">您必須指派 Exchange Online 中的權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-140">You have to assign the permissions in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-141">這是因為基礎指令程式用來搜尋稽核記錄是 Exchange Online cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-141">This is because the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an Exchange Online cmdlet.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-142">由使用者或系統管理員執行稽核的活動時，會產生稽核記錄，並且儲存在貴組織的 Office 365 稽核記錄檔中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-142">When an audited activity is performed by a user or admin, an audit record is generated and stored in the Office 365 audit log for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-143">稽核記錄會保留 （而且可搜尋稽核記錄中） 的時間長度，取決於您的 Office 365 訂閱，並特別指定給特定使用者的授權類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-143">The length of time that an audit record is retained (and searchable in the audit log) depends on your Office 365 subscription, and specifically the type of the license that is assigned to a specific user.</span></span>

     - <span data-ttu-id="279bf-144">**Office 365 E3** -稽核記錄會保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-144">**Office 365 E3** - Audit records are retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-145">這表示您可以搜尋過去 90 天內執行活動的稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-145">That means you can search the audit log for activities that were performed within the last 90 days.</span></span>

     - <span data-ttu-id="279bf-146">**Office 365 E5** -稽核記錄保留為 365 天 （一年）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-146">**Office 365 E5** - Audit records are retained for 365 days (one year).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-147">這表示您可以搜尋在過去一年內所執行的活動的稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-147">That means you can search the audit log for activities that were performed within the last year.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-148">稽核記錄保留一年的也是可用的使用者，會指派 E3/Exchange Online Plan 1 授權，而且具有 Office 365 進階合規性的附加元件授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-148">Retaining audit records for one year is also available for users that are assigned an E3/Exchange Online Plan 1 license and have an Office 365 Advanced Compliance add-on license.</span></span>

        > [!NOTE]
        > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-149">稽核記錄的一年保留期間的 E5 組織 （或 E3 有進階合規性的附加元件授權） 是目前無法使用僅做為私人預覽計畫的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-149">The one-year retention period for audit records for E5 organizations (or E3 organizations that have Advanced Compliance add-on licenses) is currently available only as part of a private preview program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-150">若要在此預覽計畫中註冊，請與[Microsoft 支援服務](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/office365/admin/contact-support-for-business-products?redirectSourcePath=%252fen-us%252farticle%252fcontact-support-for-business-products-admin-help-32a17ca7-6fa0-4870-8a8d-e25ba4ccfd4b&view=o365-worldwide&tabs=online)歸檔，並包括下列項目為您需要協助的描述: 「 長期 Office 365 稽核記錄檔私人預覽 」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-150">To enroll in this preview program, please file a request with [Microsoft Support](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/office365/admin/contact-support-for-business-products?redirectSourcePath=%252fen-us%252farticle%252fcontact-support-for-business-products-admin-help-32a17ca7-6fa0-4870-8a8d-e25ba4ccfd4b&view=o365-worldwide&tabs=online) and include the following as the description of what you need help with: "Long-term Office 365 audit log private preview".</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-151">如果您想要關閉 Office 365 中為您的組織的稽核記錄搜尋，您可以在遠端 PowerShell 連線至 Exchange Online 組織中執行下列命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-151">If you want to turn off audit log search in Office 365 for your organization, you can run the following command in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization:</span></span>
    
  ```
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $false
  ```

    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-152">若要一次開啟稽核搜尋，您可以在 Exchange Online PowerShell 中執行下列命令：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-152">To turn on audit search again, you can run the following command in Exchange Online PowerShell:</span></span>
    
  ```
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $true
  ```

    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-153">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[關閉 Office 365 中的稽核記錄搜尋](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-153">For more information, see [Turn off audit log search in Office 365](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-154">如先前所述，基礎指令程式用來搜尋稽核記錄會是 Exchange Online 指令程式，也就是**Search-unifiedauditlog**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-154">As previously stated, the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an Exchange Online cmdlet, which is **Search-UnifiedAuditLog**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-155">這表示您可以使用此指令程式來搜尋而不是使用安全性 & 合規性中心中的 [**稽核記錄搜尋**] 頁面上的 Office 365 稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-155">That means you can use this cmdlet to search the Office 365 audit log instead of using the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-156">您必須在遠端 PowerShell 連線至 Exchange Online 組織中執行此 cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-156">You have to run this cmdlet in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-157">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 < <b0>Search-unifiedauditlog</b0>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-157">For more information, see [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=834776).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-158">如果您想要以程式設計方式從 Office 365 稽核記錄檔下載資料，我們建議您使用 Office 365 管理活動 API，而不是使用 PowerShell 指令碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-158">If you want to programmatically download data from the Office 365 audit log, we recommend that you use the Office 365 Management Activity API instead of using a PowerShell script.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-159">Office 365 管理活動 API 為 REST web 服務可供您開發作業、 安全性和規範監視解決方案的組織。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-159">The Office 365 Management Activity API is a REST web service that you can use to develop operations, security, and compliance monitoring solutions for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-160">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[Office 365 管理活動 API 參考資料](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=852309)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-160">For more information, see [Office 365 Management Activity API reference](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=852309).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-161">它可以最多需要 30 分鐘或向上事件之後的 24 小時就會發生的相對應的稽核記錄項目顯示在搜尋結果中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-161">It can take up to 30 minutes or up to 24 hours after an event occurs for the corresponding audit log entry to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-162">下表顯示 Office 365 中的不同服務所花費的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-162">The following table shows the time it takes for the different services in Office 365.</span></span>
    
    |**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-163">Office 365 服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-163">Office 365 service</span></span>**|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-164">30 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-164">30 minutes</span></span>**|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-165">24 小時</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-165">24 hours</span></span>**|
    |:-----|:-----|:-----|
    |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-166">進階的威脅防護和威脅情報</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-166">Advanced Threat Protection and Threat Intelligence</span></span>  <br/> |![核取記號](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)| |
    |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-168">Azure Active Directory （使用者登入事件）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-168">Azure Active Directory (user login events)</span></span>  <br/> ||![核取記號](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> |
    |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-170">Azure Active Directory （系統事件）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-170">Azure Active Directory (admin events)</span></span>  <br/> ||![核取記號](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png) |
    |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-172">資料遺失防護</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-172">Data Loss Prevention</span></span>  <br/> |![核取記號](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)       <br/>| |

    |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-194">SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-194">SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>  <br/> |![核取記號](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> ||
    |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-196">Sway</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-196">Sway</span></span>  <br/> ||![核取記號](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> |
    |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-198">工作場所分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-198">Workplace Analytics</span></span><br/> |![核取記號](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> || 
    |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-200">Yammer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-200">Yammer</span></span>  <br/> ||![核取記號](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> |
   
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-202">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 是 Office 365 的目錄服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-202">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) is the directory service for Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-203">整合的稽核記錄檔包含使用者、 群組、 應用程式、 網域及執行在 Microsoft 365 系統管理中心，或在 Azure 中的目錄活動管理入口網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-203">The unified audit log contains user, group, application, domain, and directory activities performed in the Microsoft 365 admin center or in the in Azure management portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-204">Azure AD 事件的完整清單，請參閱[Azure Active Directory 稽核報告事件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-204">For a complete list of Azure AD events, see [Azure Active Directory Audit Report Events](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-205">Exchange Online 的稽核記錄檔包含兩種類型的事件： 在 Exchange 系統管理事件 （系統管理員所採取的動作） 與信箱事件 （在信箱上的使用者所採取的動作）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-205">Exchange Online audit logs consist of two types of events: Exchange admin events (actions taken by administrators) and mailbox events (actions taken by users on mailboxes).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-206">請注意預設未啟用信箱稽核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-206">Note that mailbox auditing isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-207">它必須啟用每個使用者信箱，才能信箱事件可以在 Office 365 稽核記錄搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-207">It must be enable for each user mailbox before mailbox events can be searched for in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-208">如需信箱稽核和信箱稽核記錄的動作的詳細資訊，請參閱 <<c0>啟用 Office 365 中的稽核的信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-208">For more information about mailbox auditing and the mailbox auditing actions that are logged, see [Enable mailbox auditing in Office 365](enable-mailbox-auditing.md).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-209">根據預設，不啟用 Power bi 的稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-209">Audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-210">若要搜尋的 Office 365 稽核記錄中的 Power BI 活動，您必須啟用 Power BI 系統管理入口網站中的稽核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-210">To search for Power BI activities in the Office 365 audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-211">如需相關指示，請參閱 < <b0>Power BI 系統管理入口網站</b0>的 「 稽核記錄 」 一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-211">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>
    
    
## <a name="search-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-212">搜尋稽核記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-212">Search the audit log</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-213">以下是在 Office 365 中搜尋稽核記錄檔的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-213">Here's the process for searching the audit log in Office 365.</span></span>
  
[<span data-ttu-id="279bf-214">步驟 1： 執行稽核記錄搜尋</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-214">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>](#step-1-run-an-audit-log-search)
  
[<span data-ttu-id="279bf-215">步驟 2： 檢視搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-215">Step 2: View the search results</span></span>](#step-2-view-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="279bf-216">步驟 3： 篩選搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-216">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="279bf-217">步驟 4： 將搜尋結果匯出至檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-217">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>](#step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file)
  
### <a name="step-1-run-an-audit-log-search"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-218">步驟 1： 執行稽核記錄搜尋</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-218">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-219">請移至 [https://compliance.microsoft.com](https://compliance.microsoft.com)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-219">Go to [https://compliance.microsoft.com](https://compliance.microsoft.com).</span></span>
    
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-220">使用私人瀏覽工作階段 （不在一般工作階段） 來存取安全性 & 合規性中心，因為這會防止您目前登入與所用的認證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-220">Use a private browsing session (not a regular session) to access the Security & Compliance Center because this will prevent the credential that you are currently logged on with from being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-221">若要開啟 [InPrivate 瀏覽工作階段在 Internet Explorer 或 Microsoft Edge 中，只需按 CTRL + SHIFT + P。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-221">To open an InPrivate Browsing session in Internet Explorer or Microsoft Edge, just press CTRL+SHIFT+P.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-222">若要在 Google Chrome （稱為 incognito 視窗） 中開啟私人瀏覽工作階段，請按 CTRL + SHIFT + N。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-222">To open a private browsing session in Google Chrome (called an incognito window), press CTRL+SHIFT+N.</span></span> 
  
2. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-223">使用公司或學校帳戶登入 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-223">Sign in to Office 365 using your work or school account.</span></span>
    
3. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-224">在安全性 & 合規性中心的左窗格中，按一下 [**搜尋**]，然後按一下 [**稽核記錄搜尋**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-224">In the left pane of the Security & Compliance Center, click **Search**, and then click **Audit log search**.</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-225">會顯示 [**稽核記錄搜尋**] 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-225">The **Audit log search** page is displayed.</span></span> 
    
    ![設定準則，然後按一下 [搜尋] 以執行報告](media/8639d09c-2843-44e4-8b4b-9f45974ff7f1.png)
  
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-227">您必須先開啟稽核記錄，才能執行稽核記錄搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-227">You have to first turn on audit logging before you can run an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-228">如果顯示 [**開始錄製使用者和系統管理員活動**] 連結，請按一下它便開啟稽核功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-228">If the **Start recording user and admin activity** link is displayed, click it to turn on auditing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-229">如果您沒有看到此連結，稽核已開啟為您的組織。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-229">If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.</span></span> 
  
4. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-230">設定下列搜尋準則：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-230">Configure the following search criteria:</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-231">a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-231">a.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-232">**活動**按一下 [下拉式清單，以顯示您可以搜尋的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-232">**Activities** Click the drop-down list to display the activities that you can search for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-233">使用者和系統管理員活動會組織的相關活動的群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-233">User and admin activities are organized in to groups of related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-234">您可以選取特定活動，或您可以按一下 [活動群組名稱來選取] 群組中的所有活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-234">You can select specific activities or you can click the activity group name to select all activities in the group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-235">您也可以按一下選取的活動，以清除選取範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-235">You can also click a selected activity to clear the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-236">執行搜尋之後，會顯示僅針對所選活動的稽核記錄項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-236">After you run the search, only the audit log entries for the selected activities are displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-237">選取 [**顯示所有活動的結果**會顯示所選取的使用者或使用者群組執行的所有活動的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-237">Selecting **Show results for all activities** will display results for all activities performed by the selected user or group of users.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-238">超過 100 個使用者和系統管理員活動登入 Office 365 稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-238">Over 100 user and admin activities are logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-239">按一下 [**稽核活動**] 索引標籤，在主題的本文，查看每個不同的 Office 365 服務中每個活動的描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-239">Click the **Audited activities** tab at the topic of this article to see the descriptions of every activity in each of the different Office 365 services.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-240">b.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-240">b.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-241">預設會選取**開始日期**和**結束日期**過去 7 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-241">**Start date** and **End date** The last seven days are selected by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-242">選取要顯示在該期間內發生的事件的日期和時間範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-242">Select a date and time range to display the events that occurred within that period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-243">日期和時間會以 Coordinated Universal Time (UTC) 格式呈現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-243">The date and time are presented in Coordinated Universal Time (UTC) format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-244">您可以指定的最大的日期範圍為 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-244">The maximum date range that you can specify is 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-245">如果選取的日期範圍大於 90 天內，會顯示錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-245">An error is displayed if the selected date range is greater than 90 days.</span></span> 
    
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-246">如果您正在使用的 90 天的最大的日期範圍，選取目前時間的**開始日期**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-246">If you're using the maximum date range of 90 days, select the current time for the **Start date**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-247">否則，您會收到錯誤訊息說明的開始日期是早於結束日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-247">Otherwise, you'll receive an error saying that the start date is earlier than the end date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-248">如果您已開啟稽核在過去 90 天內，最大的日期範圍無法啟動之前已開啟稽核的日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-248">If you've turned on auditing within the last 90 days, the maximum date range can't start before the date that auditing was turned on.</span></span> 
  
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-249">c.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-249">c.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-250">**使用者**在此方塊中按一下，然後選取 [顯示搜尋結果的一或多個使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-250">**Users** Click in this box and then select one or more users to display search results for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-251">選取您在此方塊中選取的使用者所執行的活動的稽核記錄項目會顯示在結果清單中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-251">The audit log entries for the selected activity performed by the users you select in this box are displayed in the list of results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-252">保留此方塊留白，以傳回組織中的所有使用者 （與服務帳戶） 的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-252">Leave this box blank to return entries for all users (and service accounts) in your organization.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-253">d.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-253">d.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-254">**檔案、 資料夾或網站**輸入部分或全部要搜尋的檔案的資料夾，其中包含指定的關鍵字的相關活動的檔案或資料夾名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-254">**File, folder, or site** Type some or all of a file or folder name to search for activity related to the file of folder that contains the specified keyword.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-255">您也可以指定的檔案或資料夾的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-255">You can also specify a URL of a file or folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-256">如果您使用的 URL，務必類型的完整的 URL 路徑，或如果您只需要輸入 URL，部分不會包含任何特殊字元或空格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-256">If you use a URL, be sure the type the full URL path or if you just type a portion of the URL, don't include any special characters or spaces.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-257">保留此方塊留白，以傳回組織中的所有檔案及資料夾的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-257">Leave this box blank to return entries for all files and folders in your organization.</span></span>
    
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-258">如果您要尋找與**網站**相關的所有活動，新增萬用字元符號 (\*) 之後的 URL，可傳回該網站; 的所有項目例如， \**"https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/* 」\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-258">If you're looking for all activities related to a **site**, add the wildcard symbol (\*) after the URL to return all entries for that site; for example, **"https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/\*"**.</span></span>
    
5. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-259">按一下 [**搜尋**] 以執行使用您的搜尋準則的 [搜尋]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-259">Click **Search** to run the search using your search criteria.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-260">搜尋結果會載入，且在幾分鐘之後被顯示在 [**結果**] 下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-260">The search results are loaded, and after a few moments they are displayed under **Results**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-261">搜尋完成時，會顯示找到的結果數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-261">When the search is finished, the number of results found is displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-262">請注意，將會以遞增 150 事件; 在**結果**窗格中顯示最大值為 5000 個事件如果超過 5000 筆事件符合搜尋準則，會顯示最近的 5000 個事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-262">Note that a maximum of 5,000 events will be displayed in the **Results** pane in increments of 150 events; if more than 5,000 events meet the search criteria, the most recent 5,000 events are displayed.</span></span> 
    
    ![搜尋完成之後，會顯示的結果數](media/986216f1-ca2f-4747-9480-e232b5bf094c.png)
  
  
#### <a name="tips-for-searching-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-264">搜尋稽核記錄檔的秘訣</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-264">Tips for searching the audit log</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-265">您可以選取特定活動的活動名稱上按一下來進行搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-265">You can select specific activities to search for by clicking on the activity name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-266">或者您可以在群組名稱上按一下 [搜尋群組 （例如**檔案和資料夾的活動**） 中的所有活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-266">Or you can search for all activities in a group (such as **File and folder activities**) by clicking on the group name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-267">如果選取的活動，則您可以按一下它，取消選取項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-267">If an activity is selected, you can click it to cancel the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-268">您也可以使用 [搜尋] 方塊中顯示含有您所輸入的關鍵字的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-268">You can also use the search box to display the activities that contain the keyword that you type.</span></span>
    
    ![按一下以選取所有活動的活動群組名稱](media/3cde97cb-6f35-47c0-8612-ecd9c6ac36a3.png)
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-270">您必須以顯示從 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄的事件**活動**清單中選取 [**顯示所有活動的結果**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-270">You have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list to display events from the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-271">從這個稽核記錄的事件結果中的 [**活動**] 欄中顯示的指令程式名稱 （例如， **Set-mailbox** ）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-271">Events from this audit log display a cmdlet name (for example, **Set-Mailbox** ) in the **Activity** column in the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-272">如需詳細資訊，本主題中的 [**稽核活動**] 索引標籤，然後按一下 [ **Exchange 系統管理員活動**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-272">For more information, click the **Audited activities** tab in this topic and then click **Exchange admin activities**.</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-273">同樣地，有某些稽核活動在**活動**清單中沒有對應的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-273">Similarly, there are some auditing activities that don't have a corresponding item in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-274">如果您知道這些活動的作業的名稱，您可以搜尋所有活動，然後在 [**活動**] 欄中的方塊中輸入作業的名稱來篩選結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-274">If you know the name of the operation for these activities, you can search for all activities, then filter the results by typing the name of the operation in the box for the **Activity** column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-275">請參閱[步驟 3： 篩選搜尋結果](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)如需有關篩選結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-275">See [Step 3: Filter the search results](#step-3-filter-the-search-results) for more information about filtering the results.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-276">按一下 [若要清除目前的搜尋準則的 [**清除**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-276">Click **Clear** to clear the current search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-277">日期範圍會傳回為預設的過去 7 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-277">The date range returns to the default of the last seven days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-278">您也可以按一下 [取消選取的所有活動 [**清除 [全部]，以顯示結果的所有活動**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-278">You can also click **Clear all to show results for all activities** to cancel all selected activities.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-279">如果找不到 5000 筆結果，您可能可以假設有超過 5000 筆符合搜尋準則的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-279">If 5,000 results are found, you can probably assume there are more than 5,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-280">您可以精簡搜尋準則，並重新執行搜尋以返回較少的結果，或是您可以藉由選取 [**匯出結果**匯出所有的搜尋結果\>**下載所有結果**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-280">You can either refine the search criteria and rerun the search to return fewer results, or you can export all of the search results by selecting **Export results** \> **Download all results**.</span></span>

  
### <a name="step-2-view-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-281">步驟 2： 檢視搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-281">Step 2: View the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-282">稽核記錄搜尋結果] 底下會顯示**結果**[**稽核記錄搜尋**] 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-282">The results of an audit log search are displayed under **Results** on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-283">如先前所述的遞增量 150 事件會顯示最大值為 5000 個 （最新） 的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-283">As previously stated a maximum of 5,000 (newest) events are displayed in increments of 150 events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-284">若要顯示更多事件您可以使用捲軸列在 [**結果**] 窗格中，或您可以按**Shift + End**以顯示下一步] 150 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-284">To display more events you can use the scroll bar in the **Results** pane or you can press **Shift + End** to display the next 150 events.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-285">結果包含下列搜尋傳回的每個事件的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-285">The results contain the following information about each event returned by the search.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-286">**日期：** 日期和時間 （UTC 格式） 事件發生時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-286">**Date:** The date and time (in UTC format) when the event occurred.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-287">**IP 位址：** 活動已記錄時使用的裝置 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-287">**IP address:** The IP address of the device that was used when the activity was logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-288">IP 位址會顯示在 IPv4 或 IPv6 地址格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-288">The IP address is displayed in either an IPv4 or IPv6 address format.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-289">**使用者：** 使用者 （或服務帳戶） 誰執行觸發事件的動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-289">**User:** The user (or service account) who performed the action that triggered the event.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-290">**活動：** 執行活動的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-290">**Activity:** The activity performed by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-291">此值會對應至您在 [**活動**] 下拉式清單中選取的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-291">This value corresponds to the activities that you selected in the **Activities** drop down list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-292">從 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄的事件，此欄中的值會是 Exchange 指令程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-292">For an event from the Exchange admin audit log, the value in this column is an Exchange cmdlet.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-293">**項目：** 物件已建立或修改由於相對應的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-293">**Item:** The object that was created or modified as a result of the corresponding activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-294">例如，檢視或修改的檔案或已更新的使用者帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-294">For example, the file that was viewed or modified or the user account that was updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-295">並非所有活動中此欄都有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-295">Not all activities have a value in this column.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-296">**詳細資料：** 關於活動的額外詳細資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-296">**Detail:** Additional detail about an activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-297">同樣地，並非所有活動會都有一個值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-297">Again, not all activities will have a value.</span></span> 
    
> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-298">按一下欄標題來排序結果的**結果**下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-298">Click a column header under **Results** to sort the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-299">您可以排序結果從 A 到 Z 或 Z A 按一下 「**日期**」 標題來排序結果的最舊到最新或最新到最舊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-299">You can sort the results from A to Z or Z to A. Click the **Date** header to sort the results from oldest to newest or newest to oldest.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="view-the-details-for-a-specific-event"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-300">檢視特定事件的詳細資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-300">View the details for a specific event</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-301">您可以檢視事件有關的更多詳細資料]，即可在搜尋結果清單中的事件記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-301">You can view more details about an event by clicking the event record in the list of search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-302">**詳細資料**] 頁面會顯示包含從事件記錄的詳細的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-302">A **Details** page is displayed that contains the detailed properties from the event record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-303">會顯示的內容取決於 Office 365 服務發生事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-303">The properties that are displayed depend on the Office 365 service in which the event occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-304">若要顯示這些詳細資料，請按一下 [**更多的資訊**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-304">To display these details, click **More information**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-305">如需說明，請參閱[在 Office 365 的詳細的內容稽核記錄](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-305">For descriptions, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>
  
![按一下 [檢視稽核記錄的事件記錄的詳細的內容的詳細資訊](media/6df582ae-d339-4735-b1a6-80914fb77a08.png)

  
### <a name="step-3-filter-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-307">步驟 3： 篩選搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-307">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-308">除了排序，您也可以篩選稽核記錄搜尋的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-308">In addition to sorting, you can also filter the results of an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-309">這是個不錯的功能，可協助您快速篩選特定使用者或活動的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-309">This is a great feature that can help you quickly filter the results for a specific user or activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-310">您可以一開始建立整體搜尋，並快速篩選結果，以查看特定的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-310">You can initially create a wide search and then quickly filter the results to see specific events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-311">然後您可以縮小搜尋準則，並重新執行搜尋以返回較小，更簡潔的結果集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-311">Then you can narrow the search criteria and re-run the search to return a smaller, more concise set of results.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-312">若要篩選的結果：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-312">To filter the results:</span></span>
  
1. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-313">執行稽核記錄搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-313">Run an audit log search.</span></span>
    
2. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-314">結果會顯示，按一下 [**篩選結果**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-314">When the results are displayed, click **Filter results**.</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-315">關鍵字方塊會顯示在每個資料行標題之下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-315">Keyword boxes are displayed under each column header.</span></span>
    
3. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-316">按一下其中一個方塊下欄標題，然後輸入單字或片語，視您正在篩選的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-316">Click one of the boxes under a column header and type a word or phrase, depending on the column you're filtering on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-317">結果會以動態方式重新調整以顯示符合篩選的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-317">The results will dynamically readjust to display the events that match your filter.</span></span>
    
    ![輸入字詞的篩選，以顯示符合篩選的事件](media/542dc323-a997-402c-934b-cc5e218e50bc.png)
  
4. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-319">若要清除篩選，請按一下 [篩選] 方塊中的**X**或只要按一下 [**隱藏篩選**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-319">To clear a filter, click the **X** in the filter box or just click **Hide filtering**.</span></span>
    
> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-320">若要顯示來自 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄的事件，請輸入**-**（虛線） 在 [**活動**篩選] 方塊中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-320">To display events from the Exchange admin audit log, type a **-** (dash) in the **Activity** filter box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-321">這會顯示指令程式名稱，會顯示在 Exchange 系統事件的 [**活動**] 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-321">This will display cmdlet names, which are displayed in the **Activity** column for Exchange admin events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-322">然後您可以排序依字母順序排列的指令程式名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-322">Then you can sort the cmdlet names in alphabetical order.</span></span> 

### <a name="step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-323">步驟 4： 將搜尋結果匯出至檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-323">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-324">您可以將稽核記錄搜尋結果匯出至本機電腦上的逗點分隔的值 (CSV) 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-324">You can export the results of an audit log search to a comma separated value (CSV) file on your local computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-325">您可以在 Microsoft Excel 中開啟此檔案，並使用多個資料行到功能，例如搜尋，排序、 篩選及分割的單一資料行 （包含多重值的儲存格）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-325">You can open this file in Microsoft Excel and use features such as search, sorting, filtering, and splitting a single column (that contains multi-value cells) into multiple columns.</span></span>
  
1. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-326">執行稽核記錄搜尋]，然後再修訂的搜尋準則，直到您有想要的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-326">Run an audit log search, and then revise the search criteria until you have the desired results.</span></span>
    
2. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-327">按一下 [**匯出結果**，選取下列選項之一：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-327">Click **Export results** and select one of the following options:</span></span> 
    
  - <span data-ttu-id="279bf-328">**儲存載入結果**選擇此選項可匯出] 底下**的結果**會顯示的項目 \* \* 稽核記錄搜尋 \* \*] 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-328">**Save loaded results** Choose this option to export only the entries that are displayed under **Results** on the \*\* Audit log search \*\* page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-329">下載的 CSV 檔案包含 （日期、 使用者、 活動、 項目，以及詳細資料） 頁面上顯示的相同資料行 （和資料）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-329">The CSV file that is downloaded contains the same columns (and data) displayed on the page (Date, User, Activity, Item, and Details).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-330">（名為**多個**） 額外一欄包含在 CSV 檔案包含稽核記錄項目從的詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-330">An additional column (named **More**) is included in the CSV file that contains more information from the audit log entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-331">因為您要匯出相同的結果載入 （與檢視） 的最大值為 5000 的項目會匯出在 [**稽核記錄搜尋**] 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-331">Because you're exporting the same results that are loaded (and viewable) on the **Audit log search** page, a maximum of 5,000 entries are exported.</span></span> 
    
  - <span data-ttu-id="279bf-332">**下載所有結果**選擇此選項以從符合搜尋準則的 Office 365 稽核記錄檔匯出所有的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-332">**Download all results** Choose this option to export all entries from the Office 365 audit log that meet the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-333">一組大型的搜尋結果，選擇此選項以從除了 5000 筆結果，可以顯示在 [**稽核記錄搜尋**] 頁面上的稽核記錄檔下載所有項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-333">For a large set of search results, choose this option to download all entries from the audit log in addition to the 5,000 results that can be displayed on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-334">此選項將稽核記錄檔從下載的未經處理資料至 CSV 檔案，並包含名為**AuditData**] 欄中的稽核記錄項目中的其他資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-334">This option will download the raw data from the audit log to a CSV file, and contains additional information from the audit log entry in a column named **AuditData**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-335">可能需要較長的時間下載檔案，如果您選擇此匯出選項，因為可能遠大於一如果您選擇其他選項下載的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-335">It may take longer to download the file if you choose this export option because the file may be much larger than the one that's downloaded if you choose the other option.</span></span>
    
    > [!IMPORTANT]
    > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-336">您可以下載至 CSV 檔案的最大值為 50000 的項目從單一的稽核記錄搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-336">You can download a maximum of 50,000 entries to a CSV file from a single audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-337">如果 50000 的項目會下載到 CSV 檔案，您可能可以假設有超過 50000 個符合搜尋準則的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-337">If 50,000 entries are downloaded to the CSV file, you can probably assume there are more than 50,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-338">若要匯出超過此限制，請嘗試使用日期範圍，以減少稽核記錄項目的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-338">To export more than this limit, try using a date range to reduce the number of audit log entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-339">您可能使用較小的日期範圍，若要匯出超過 50000 個項目執行多個搜尋。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-339">You might have to run multiple searches with smaller date ranges to export more than 50,000 entries.</span></span> 
  
3. <span data-ttu-id="279bf-340">選取 [匯出] 選項後，會提示您開啟 CSV 檔案，將它儲存到 [下載項目] 資料夾中，或將其儲存至特定資料夾視窗的底部會顯示訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-340">After you select an export option, a message is displayed at the bottom of the window that prompts you to open the CSV file, save it to the Downloads folder, or save it to a specific folder.</span></span>

  
#### <a name="more-information-about-exporting-audit-log-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-341">匯出稽核記錄搜尋結果的詳細資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-341">More information about exporting audit log search results</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-342">**下載所有結果**] 選項會下載到 CSV 檔案從 Office 365 稽核記錄檔的未經處理資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-342">The **Download all results** option downloads the raw data from the Office 365 audit log to a CSV file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-343">此檔案包含不同的資料行名稱 （CreationDate、 UserIds、 作業、 AuditData） 比如果您選取 [**儲存載入結果**] 選項已下載的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-343">This file contains different column names (CreationDate, UserIds, Operation, AuditData) than the file that's downloaded if you select the **Save loaded results** option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-344">兩個不同的 CSV 檔案的相同活動中的值也可能會不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-344">The values in the two different CSV files for the same activity may also be different.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-345">例如，在 csv 檔案中的 [**動作**] 欄中的活動檔案，且可能會有不同的值會顯示在 [**稽核記錄搜尋**] 頁面上; 中的 [**活動**] 欄中的 「 好記易懂 「 版本例如，MailboxLogin 相對於使用者登入至信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-345">For example, the activity in the **Action** column in the CSV file and may have a different value than the "user-friendly" version that's displayed in the **Activity** column on the **Audit log search** page; for example, MailboxLogin vs. User signed in to mailbox.</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-346">如果您要下載所有結果，CSV 檔案中包含名為**AuditData**，其中包含每個事件相關的其他資訊的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-346">If you download all results, the CSV file contains a column named **AuditData**, which contains additional information about each event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-347">如先前所述，此欄會包含多個屬性的稽核記錄檔記錄的多重值屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-347">As previously stated, this column contains a multi-value property for multiple properties from the audit log record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-348">此多重值屬性中的**屬性： 值**組的每個都以逗號分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-348">Each of the **property:value** pairs in this multi-value property are separated by a comma.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-349">您可以使用 Excel 中的 Power Query 此資料行分割成多個資料行，使每個屬性將有它自己的資料行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-349">You can use the Power Query in Excel to split this column into multiple columns so that each property will have its own column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-350">這可讓您排序及篩選一或多個這些屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-350">This will let you sort and filter on one or more of these properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-351">若要了解如何執行這項操作，請參閱[分割資料行的文字 (Power Query)](https://support.office.com/article/5282d425-6dd0-46ca-95bf-8e0da9539662)的 「 分割資料行分隔符號 」 一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-351">To learn how to do this, see the "Split a column by delimiter" section in [Split a column of text (Power Query)](https://support.office.com/article/5282d425-6dd0-46ca-95bf-8e0da9539662).</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-352">分割**AuditData**欄之後，您可以篩選以顯示特定類型的活動的詳細的內容的 [**作業**] 欄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-352">After you split the **AuditData** column, you can filter on the **Operations** column to display the detailed properties for a specific type of activity.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-353">沒有 3,060 字元會顯示在稽核記錄的**AuditData**欄位的資料的長度限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-353">There's a 3,060-character limit for the data that's displayed in the **AuditData** field for an audit record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-354">如果超出 3,060 字元限制，則此欄位中的資料會捨去成整數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-354">If the 3,060-character limit is exceeded, the data in this field is truncated.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-355">當您下載所有結果包含的事件來自不同 Office 365 服務的搜尋查詢時，CSV 檔案中的 [ **AuditData** ] 欄會包含不同根據服務巨集指令執行中的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-355">When you download all results from a search query that contains events from different Office 365 services, the **AuditData** column in the CSV file contains different properties depending on which service the action was performed in.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-356">例如，從 Exchange 和 Azure AD 的稽核記錄項目包含名為**ResultStatus**表示動作是否成功與否屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-356">For example, entries from Exchange and Azure AD audit logs include a property named **ResultStatus** that indicates if the action was successful or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-357">此屬性不包含在 SharePoint 中的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-357">This property isn't included for events in SharePoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-358">同樣地，SharePoint 事件有屬性，識別的網站 URL 的檔案和資料夾相關的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-358">Similarly, SharePoint events have a property that identifies the site URL for file and folder related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-359">若要降低此行為，請考慮使用不同的搜尋從單一服務匯出活動的結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-359">To mitigate this behavior, consider using different searches to export the results for activities from a single service.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="279bf-360">當您下載所有的結果，以及服務每一個 CSV 檔案中的 [ **AuditData** ] 欄中所列的屬性描述一套用於，請參閱[在 Office 365 的詳細的內容稽核記錄](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-360">For a description of the properties that are listed in the **AuditData** column in the CSV file when you download all results, and the service each one applies to, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

## <a name="audited-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-361">稽核的活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-361">Audited activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-362">本節中的表格說明稽核 Office 365 中的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-362">The tables in this section describe the activities that are audited in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-363">您可以藉由在安全性與合規性中心搜尋稽核記錄搜尋這些事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-363">You can search for these events by searching the audit log in the security and compliance center.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-364">這些表格群組相關的活動或從特定的 Office 365 服務的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-364">These tables group related activities or the activities from a specific Office 365 service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-365">表格包含 [**活動**] 下拉式清單中顯示的易記名稱及對應的作業，當您匯出搜尋結果出現在稽核記錄的詳細資訊和 CSV 檔案的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-365">The tables include the friendly name that's displayed in the **Activities** drop-down list and the name of the corresponding operation that appears in the detailed information of an audit record and in the CSV file when you export the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-366">如需詳細資訊的說明，請參閱[在 Office 365 的詳細的內容稽核記錄](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-366">For descriptions of the detailed information, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

### <a name="file-and-page-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-389">檔案和] 頁面上的活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-389">File and page activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-390">下表說明 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的檔案和頁面活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-390">The following table describes the file and page activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>
  
|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-391">易記名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-391">Friendly name</span></span>**|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-392">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-392">Operation</span></span>**|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-393">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-393">Description</span></span>**|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-394">存取的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-394">Accessed file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-395">FileAccessed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-395">FileAccessed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-396">使用者或系統帳戶存取檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-396">User or system account accesses a file.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-397">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-397">(none)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-398">FileAccessedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-398">FileAccessedExtended</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-399">這與 「 存取檔案 」 (FileAccessed) 活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-399">This is related to the "Accessed file" (FileAccessed) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-400">相同的人持續存取檔案的一段時間 （最多 3 小時） 時，會記錄 FileAccessedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-400">A FileAccessedExtended event is logged when the same person continually accesses a file for an extended period of time (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-401">記錄 FileAccessedExtended 事件的目的是要減少 FileAccessed 事件持續存取檔案時所記錄的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-401">The purpose of logging FileAccessedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileAccessed events that are logged when a file is continually accessed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-402">這可協助降低的多個 FileAccessed 記錄功能基本上是相同的雜訊使用者活動，並可讓您專注於初始 （和更重要） FileAccessed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-402">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileAccessed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileAccessed event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-403">存回檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-403">Checked in file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-404">FileCheckedIn</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-404">FileCheckedIn</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-405">使用者存回他們從文件庫取出的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-405">User checks in a document that they checked out from a document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-406">取出檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-406">Checked out file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-407">FileCheckedOut</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-407">FileCheckedOut</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-408">使用者取出的文件庫中的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-408">User checks out a document located in a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-409">使用者可以簽出，並與他們共用的文件進行變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-409">Users can check out and make changes to documents that have been shared with them.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-410">複製的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-410">Copied file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-411">FileCopied</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-411">FileCopied</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-412">使用者會複製網站中的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-412">User copies a document from a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-413">複製的檔案可以儲存到網站上的另一個資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-413">The copied file can be saved to another folder on the site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-414">已刪除的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-414">Deleted file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-415">FileDeleted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-415">FileDeleted</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-416">使用者從網站刪除文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-416">User deletes a document from a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-417">資源回收筒中已刪除的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-417">Deleted file from recycle bin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-418">FileDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-418">FileDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-419">使用者從網站的資源回收筒刪除檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-419">User deletes a file from the recycle bin of a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-420">第二階段資源回收筒中已刪除的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-420">Deleted file from second-stage recycle bin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-421">FileDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-421">FileDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-422">使用者從網站的第二階段資源回收筒刪除檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-422">User deletes a file from the second-stage recycle bin of a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-423">在檔案中偵測到惡意程式碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-423">Detected malware in file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-424">FileMalwareDetected</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-424">FileMalwareDetected</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-425">SharePoint 防毒引擎偵測惡意程式碼檔案中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-425">SharePoint anti-virus engine detects malware in a file.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-426">已捨棄的檔案簽出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-426">Discarded file checkout</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-427">FileCheckOutDiscarded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-427">FileCheckOutDiscarded</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-p154">使用者捨棄 (或復原) 取出的檔案。這表示對取出的文件所做的任何變更會被捨棄，不儲存到文件庫中的文件版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-p154">User discards (or undos) a checked out file. That means any changes they made to the file when it was checked out are discarded, and not saved to the version of the document in the document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-430">下載的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-430">Downloaded file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-431">FileDownloaded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-431">FileDownloaded</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-432">使用者從網站下載的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-432">User downloads a document from a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-433">修改的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-433">Modified file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-434">FileModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-434">FileModified</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-435">使用者或系統帳戶修改的內容或位在網站上的文件的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-435">User or system account modifies the content or the properties of a document located on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-436">(無)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-436">(none)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-437">FileModifiedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-437">FileModifiedExtended</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-438">這與 「 最後修改檔案 」 (FileModified) 活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-438">This is related to the "Modified file" (FileModified) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-439">同一人士不斷修改檔案的一段時間 （最多 3 小時） 時，會記錄 FileModifiedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-439">A FileModifiedExtended event is logged when the same person continually modifies a file for an extended period of time (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-440">記錄 FileModifiedExtended 事件的目的是減少不斷修改檔案時，會記錄的 FileModified 事件的次數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-440">The purpose of logging FileModifiedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileModified events that are logged when a file is continually modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-441">這可協助降低的多個 FileModified 記錄功能基本上是相同的雜訊使用者活動，並可讓您專注於初始 （和更重要） FileModified 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-441">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileModified records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileModified event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-442">移動的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-442">Moved file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-443">FileMoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-443">FileMoved</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-444">使用者從其目前的位置，網站上的新位置，移動文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-444">User moves a document from its current location on a site to a new location.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-445">Recycled 檔案的所有次要版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-445">Recycled all minor versions of file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-446">FileVersionsAllMinorsRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-446">FileVersionsAllMinorsRecycled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-447">使用者從檔案的版本歷程記錄刪除所有的次要版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-447">User deletes all minor versions from the version history of a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-448">已刪除的版本會移至網站資源回收筒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-448">The deleted versions are moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-449">Recycled 檔案的所有版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-449">Recycled all versions of file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-450">FileVersionsAllRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-450">FileVersionsAllRecycled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-451">使用者從檔案的版本歷程記錄刪除所有版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-451">User deletes all versions from the version history of a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-452">已刪除的版本會移至網站資源回收筒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-452">The deleted versions are moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-453">回收的檔案版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-453">Recycled version of file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-454">FileVersionRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-454">FileVersionRecycled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-455">使用者從檔案的版本歷程記錄刪除版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-455">User deletes a version from the version history of a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-456">已刪除的版本會移至網站資源回收筒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-456">The deleted version is moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-457">重新命名的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-457">Renamed file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-458">FileRenamed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-458">FileRenamed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-459">使用者重新命名的網站上的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-459">User renames a document on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="sharing-and-access-request-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-509">共用和存取要求活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-509">Sharing and access request activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-510">下表說明 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的使用者共用及存取要求活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-510">The following table describes the user sharing and access request activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-511">共用事件，在 [**結果**] 下的 [**詳細資料**] 欄會識別的使用者或群組共用的項目名稱，以及是否該使用者或群組為成員或組織中的來賓。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-511">For sharing events, the **Detail** column under **Results** identifies the name of the user or group the item was shared with and whether that user or group is a member or guest in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-512">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 <<c0>使用 Office 365 稽核記錄檔中的共用稽核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-512">For more information, see [Use sharing auditing in the Office 365 audit log](use-sharing-auditing.md).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-513">使用者可以成為 [*成員*] 或 [*訪客*的使用者物件的 UserType 屬性為基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-513">Users can be either  *members*  or  *guests*  based on the UserType property of the user object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-514">成員通常員工，而來賓通常是組織外的一目了然。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-514">A member is usually an employee, and a guest is usually a collaborator outside of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-515">當使用者可接受的共用邀請 （且已不是您組織的一部分） 時，就會為他們來賓帳戶建立貴組織的目錄中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-515">When a user accepts a sharing invitation (and isn't already part of your organization), a guest account is created for them in your organization's directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-516">一旦來賓使用者帳戶目錄中，可能會直接與他們共用資源，（而不需要邀請）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-516">Once the guest user has an account in your directory, resources may be shared directly with them (without requiring an invitation).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-523">公認的共用邀請</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-523">Accepted sharing invitation</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-524">SharingInvitationAccepted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-524">SharingInvitationAccepted</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-525">使用者 （成員或來賓） 接受的共用邀請，並已授與給資源的存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-525">User (member or guest) accepted a sharing invitation and was granted access to a resource.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-526">此事件資訊包含獲邀使用者與用來接受邀請的電子郵件地址 （它們可能會不同）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-526">This event includes information about the user who was invited and the email address that was used to accept the invitation (they could be different).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-527">這項活動通常伴隨告訴您，如何已授與使用者存取的資源，例如，將使用者新增至具有存取的資源群組的第二個事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-527">This activity is often accompanied by a second event that describes how the user was granted access to the resource, for example, adding the user to a group that has access to the resource.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-534">封鎖的共用邀請</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-534">Blocked sharing invitation</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-535">SharingInvitationBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-535">SharingInvitationBlocked</span></span>  <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="279bf-536">因為 [允許] 或 [拒絕外部共用的目標使用者的網域為基礎的外部共用原則封鎖您組織中的使用者所傳送的共用邀請。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-536">A sharing invitation sent by a user in your organization is blocked because of an external sharing policy that either allows or denies external sharing based on the domain of the target user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-537">在此情況下，共用邀請，所以封鎖郵件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-537">In this case, the sharing invitation was blocked because:</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="279bf-538">允許的網域清單不包含目標使用者的網域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-538">The target user's domain isn't included in the list of allowed domains.</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="279bf-539">Or</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-539">Or</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="279bf-540">目標使用者的網域包含在封鎖網域清單中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-540">The target user's domain is included in the list of blocked domains.</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="279bf-541">如需允許或封鎖的網域為基礎的外部共用的詳細資訊，請參閱 < <b0>SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中共用的受限的網域</b0>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-541">For more information about allowing or blocking external sharing based on domains, see [Restricted domains sharing in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business](https://support.office.com/article/5d7589cd-0997-4a00-a2ba-2320ec49c4e9).</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-604">使用匿名的連結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-604">Used an anonymous link</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-605">AnonymousLinkUsed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-605">AnonymousLinkUsed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-606">匿名使用者會使用匿名的連結，以存取資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-606">An anonymous user accessed a resource by using an anonymous link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-607">使用者的身分識別可能是未知的但您可以取得其他詳細資料，例如使用者的 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-607">The user's identity might be unknown, but you can get other details such as the user's IP address.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-608">取消共用的檔案、 資料夾或網站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-608">Unshared file, folder, or site</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-609">SharingRevoked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-609">SharingRevoked</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-610">使用者 （成員或來賓） 取消共用檔案、 資料夾或先前已與另一位使用者共用的網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-610">User (member or guest) unshared a file, folder, or site that was previously shared with another user.</span></span>  <br/> |
