### <a name="synchronization-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-626">同步處理活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-626">Synchronization activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-627">下表列出 SharePoint Online 和商務用 OneDrive 中的檔案同步處理活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-627">The following table lists file synchronization activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>
  
|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-628">易記名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-628">Friendly name</span></span>**|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-629">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-629">Operation</span></span>**|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-630">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-630">Description</span></span>**|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-631">允許電腦同步處理檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-631">Allowed computer to sync files</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-632">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-632">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-633">使用者成功建立與網站的同步處理關係。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-633">User successfully establishes a sync relationship with a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-634">同步處理關係是成功，因為使用者的電腦所新增的網域 （稱為 「*安全的收件者清單*） 可以存取您組織中的文件庫清單到網域的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-634">The sync relationship is successful because the user's computer is a member of a domain that's been added to the list of domains (called the  *safe recipients list*  ) that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-635">如需此功能的詳細資訊，請參閱 <<c0>使用 Windows PowerShell cmdlet 來啟用的網域已在安全收件者清單中的 OneDrive 同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-635">For more information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-636">封鎖電腦進行同步處理檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-636">Blocked computer from syncing files</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-637">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-637">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-638">使用者嘗試建立的網站不是貴組織的網域的成員電腦同步處理關係或是尚未新增至清單中網域的網域的成員 (稱為 「*安全收件者清單)* ，可以存取文件在您的組織中的文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-638">User tries to establish a sync relationship with a site from a computer that isn't a member of your organization's domain or is a member of a domain that hasn't been added to the list of domains (called the  *safe recipients list)*  that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-639">不允許同步處理關係，以及使用者的電腦會封鎖同步處理、 下載，或上傳的文件庫的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-639">The sync relationship is not allowed, and the user's computer is blocked from syncing, downloading, or uploading files on a document library.</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-640">如需此功能的資訊，請參閱 <<c0>使用 Windows PowerShell cmdlet 來啟用的網域已在安全收件者清單中的 OneDrive 同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-640">For information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-641">下載至電腦的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-641">Downloaded files to computer</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-642">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-642">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-643">使用者建立同步處理關係並且成功下載檔案第一次至其電腦從文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-643">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully downloads files for the first time to their computer from a document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-644">下載的檔案，變更至電腦</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-644">Downloaded file changes to computer</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-645">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-645">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-646">使用者成功的任何變更檔案從下載的文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-646">User successfully downloads any changes to files from a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-647">這項活動會指出文件庫中的檔案所做的任何變更已下載至使用者的電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-647">This activity indicates that any changes that were made to files in the document library were downloaded to the user's computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-648">因為 （如**下載至電腦的檔案**活動所指示） 先前的文件庫下載的使用者，已下載只變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-648">Only changes were downloaded because the document library was previously downloaded by the user (as indicated by the **Downloaded files to computer** activity).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-649">上傳的檔案至文件庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-649">Uploaded files to document library</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-650">FileSyncUploadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-650">FileSyncUploadedFull</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-651">使用者建立同步處理關係並且成功將檔案上傳至文件庫第一次從其電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-651">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully uploads files for the first time from their computer to a document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-652">將變更上傳的檔案至文件庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-652">Uploaded file changes to document library</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-653">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-653">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-654">使用者成功地將變更上載至文件庫上的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-654">User successfully uploads changes to files on a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-655">此事件表示對文件庫檔案的本機版本所做的任何變更都已成功上傳至文件庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-655">This event indicates that any changes made to the local version of a file from a document library are successfully uploaded to the document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-656">只變更會卸載，因為這些檔案先前上傳的使用者 (所指示 \* \* 檔案上傳至文件庫 \* \* 活動)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-656">Only changes are unloaded because those files were previously uploaded by the user (as indicated by the \*\* Uploaded files to document library \*\* activity).</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="site-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-657">網站管理活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-657">Site administration activities</span></span>

|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-659">易記名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-659">Friendly name</span></span>**|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-660">作業</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-660">Operation</span></span>**|**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-661">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-661">Description</span></span>**|

|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-679">允許使用者建立群組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-679">Allowed user to create groups</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-680">AllowGroupCreationSet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-680">AllowGroupCreationSet</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-681">網站管理員或擁有者會新增至網站，可讓使用者權限等級指派該權限建立該網站的群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-681">Site administrator or owner adds a permission level to a site that allows a user assigned that permission to create a group for that site.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="exchange-mailbox-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-786">Exchange 信箱活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-786">Exchange mailbox activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-787">下表列出的活動，可記錄信箱稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-787">The following table lists the activities that can be logged by mailbox audit logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-788">會記錄信箱擁有者、 委派的使用者或系統管理員所執行的信箱活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-788">Mailbox activities performed by the mailbox owner, a delegated user, or an administrator are logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-789">根據預設，Office 365 中的信箱稽核無法開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-789">By default, mailbox auditing in Office 365 isn't turned on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-790">信箱稽核記錄必須開啟每一個信箱將會記錄信箱活動之前。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-790">Mailbox audit logging must be turned on for each mailbox before mailbox activity will be logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-791">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 <<c0>啟用 Office 365 中的稽核的信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-791">For more information, see [Enable mailbox auditing in Office 365](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=626109).</span></span>

### <a name="sway-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-860">Sway 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-860">Sway activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-861">下表列出在 Sway 中的使用者和系統管理員活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-861">The following table lists user and admin activities in Sway.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-862">Sway 是 Office 365 應用程式，可協助使用者收集、 格式化及分享想法、 故事，並在互動式、 web 式畫布上的簡報。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-862">Sway is an Office 365 app that helps users gather, format, and share ideas, stories, and presentations on an interactive, web-based canvas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-863">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[常見問題集關於 Sway-系統管理說明](https://support.office.com/article/446380fa-25bf-47b2-996c-e12cb2f9d075)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-863">For more information, see [Frequently asked questions about Sway - Admin Help](https://support.office.com/article/446380fa-25bf-47b2-996c-e12cb2f9d075).</span></span>

### <a name="application-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-965">應用程式管理活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-965">Application administration activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-966">下表列出會記錄系統管理員新增或變更在 Azure AD 中註冊應用程式時的應用程式系統管理員活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-966">The following table lists application admin activities that are logged when an admin adds or changes an application that's registered in Azure AD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-967">任何依賴進行驗證的 Azure AD 的應用程式必須在目錄中註冊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-967">Any application that relies on Azure AD for authentication must be registered in the directory.</span></span>

### <a name="ediscovery-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1053">電子文件探索活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1053">eDiscovery activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1054">內容搜尋和 eDiscovery 相關的活動而執行的安全性與合規性中心，或藉由執行 PowerShell 的對應的稽核記錄中記錄指令程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1054">Content Search and eDiscovery-related activities that are performed in the security and compliance center or by running the corresponding PowerShell cmdlets are logged in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1055">這包括下列活動：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1055">This includes the following activities:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1056">建立及管理 eDiscovery 案例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1056">Creating and managing eDiscovery cases</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1057">建立、 啟動和編輯內容搜尋</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1057">Creating, starting, and editing Content Searches</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1058">執行內容搜尋動作，例如預覽，匯出，以及刪除搜尋結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1058">Performing Content Search actions, such as previewing, exporting, and deleting search results</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1059">設定內容搜尋的權限篩選</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1059">Configuring permissions filtering for Content Search</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1060">管理 eDiscovery 系統管理員角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1060">Managing the eDiscovery Administrator role</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1061">清單與電子文件探索活動所記錄的詳細的說明，請參閱[搜尋 eDiscovery 活動在 Office 365 稽核記錄](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1061">For a list and detailed description of the eDiscovery activities that are logged, see [Search for eDiscovery activities in the Office 365 audit log](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1062">花費最多 30 分鐘所得列在 [**活動**下拉式清單中要顯示在搜尋結果中的**eDiscovery 活動**之下的活動的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1062">It takes up to 30 minutes for events that result from the activities listed under **eDiscovery activities** in the **Activities** drop-down list to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1063">相反地，採用 24 小時的時間從 eDiscovery 對應事件的指令程式的活動，以顯示在搜尋結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1063">Conversely, it takes up to 24 hours for the corresponding events from eDiscovery cmdlet activities to appear in the search results.</span></span> 
  
### <a name="power-bi-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1064">Power BI 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1064">Power BI activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1065">您可以在 Power BI 中搜尋活動的稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1065">You can search the audit log for activities in Power BI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1066">Power BI 活動的相關資訊，請參閱[稽核組織內使用](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-auditing#activities-audited-by-power-bi)的 「 活動的稽核依 Power Power BI 」 一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1066">For information about Power BI activities, see the "Activities audited by Power Power BI" section in [Using auditing within your organization](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-auditing#activities-audited-by-power-bi).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1067">請注意，預設為未啟用 Power bi 的稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1067">Note that audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1068">若要搜尋的 Office 365 稽核記錄中的 Power BI 活動，您必須啟用 Power BI 系統管理入口網站中的稽核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1068">To search for Power BI activities in the Office 365 audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1069">如需相關指示，請參閱 < <b0>Power BI 系統管理入口網站</b0>的 「 稽核記錄 」 一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1069">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>
  
### <a name="microsoft-workplace-analytics-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1070">Microsoft 工作場所分析活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1070">Microsoft Workplace Analytics activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1071">工作場所分析提供深入群組跨 Office 365 組織的共同作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1071">Workplace Analytics provides insight into how groups collaborate across your Office 365 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1072">下表列出 「 管理員 」 角色或 「 工作場所分析中的分析師角色指派的使用者所執行的活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1072">The following table lists activities performed by users that are assigned the Administrator role or the Analyst roles in Workplace Analytics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1073">指派分析師角色的使用者擁有完整存取權的所有服務功能，以及使用產品進行分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1073">Users assigned the Analyst role have full access to all service features and use the product to do analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1074">指派系統管理員角色的使用者可以設定隱私權設定與系統的預設值，可以準備、 上傳，並確認工作場所分析中的組織資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1074">Users assigned the Administrator role can configure privacy settings and system defaults, and can prepare, upload, and verify organizational data in Workplace Analytics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1075">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 <<c0>工作場所分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1075">For more information, see [Workplace Analytics](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/workplace-analytics/index-orig).</span></span>

images**).</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1157">-啟用或停用該功能適用於使用 Microsoft Teams 聊天和通道 (**全組織 bot**) 中的 bot 的小組成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1157">- bot這不包含 T-Bot，也就是當組織 (**個別 bot**) 啟用 bot 是可用的 Teams 說明 bot。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1158">- Enables specific bots for Microsoft Teams; this doesn't include the T-Bot, which is Teams help bot that's available when bots are enabled for the organization ( **Individual bots**).</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1159">-啟用或停用若要新增分機或索引標籤 （**分機或索引標籤**） 的小組成員的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1159">- Enables or disables the ability for team members to add extensions or tabs ( **Extensions or tabs**).</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1160">-啟用或停用的 Microsoft Teams ( **Bot 端載入**) 的專屬 Bot 端載入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1160">- Enables or disables the side-loading of ### <a name="yammer-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1214">Yammer 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1214">Yammer activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1215">下表列出使用者並登入 Office 365 的系統管理員活動 Yammer 中的稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1215">The following table lists the user and admin activities in Yammer that are logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1216">若要傳回 Yammer 相關的活動，從 Office 365 稽核記錄，您必須在**活動**清單中選取 [**顯示所有活動的結果**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1216">To return Yammer-related activities from the Office 365 audit log, you have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1217">使用日期範圍] 方塊和 [**使用者**] 清單來縮小搜尋結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1217">Use the date range boxes and the **Users** list to narrow the search results.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1261">共用的檔案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1261">Shared file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1262">FileShared</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1262">FileShared</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1263">使用者與其他使用者共用檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1263">User shares a file with another user.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1264">擱置的網路使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1264">Suspended network user</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1265">NetworkUserSuspended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1265">NetworkUserSuspended</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1266">網路或已驗證的系統管理員擱置 （停用） Yammer 中的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1266">Network or verified admin suspends (deactivates) a user from Yammer.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1267">暫停的使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1267">Suspended user</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1268">UserSuspension</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1268">UserSuspension</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1269">暫停使用者帳戶 （停用）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1269">User account is suspended (deactivated).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1270">更新的檔案的描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1270">Updated file description</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1271">FileUpdateDescription</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1271">FileUpdateDescription</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1272">會在使用者變更檔案的描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1272">User changes the description of a file.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="microsoft-flow-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1279">Microsoft Flow 活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1279">Microsoft Flow activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1280">您可以在 Microsoft Flow 中搜尋活動的稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1280">You can search the audit log for activities in Microsoft Flow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1281">這些活動包括建立、 編輯和刪除流程，以及變更流程權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1281">These activities include creating, editing and deleting flows, and changing flow permissions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1282">如需流程活動的稽核資訊，請參閱 < 部落格<b0>Microsoft Flow 稽核安全性 &amp; 合規性中心中目前可用的事件</b0>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1282">For information about auditing for Flow activities, see the blog  [Microsoft Flow audit events now available in Security & Compliance Center](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/security-and-compliance-center).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-powerapps"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1283">Microsoft PowerApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1283">Microsoft PowerApps</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1284">您可以在 PowerApps 中搜尋應用程式相關的活動的稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1284">You can search the audit log for app-related activities in PowerApps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1285">這些活動包括建立、 啟動和發佈應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1285">These activities include creating, launching, and publishing an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1286">也稽核指派權限給應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1286">Assigning permissions to apps is also audited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1287">所有 PowerApps 活動的說明，請參閱[PowerApps 記錄活動](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/power-platform/admin/logging-powerapps#what-events-are-audited)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1287">For a description of all PowerApps activities, see [Activity logging for PowerApps](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/power-platform/admin/logging-powerapps#what-events-are-audited).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-stream-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1288">Microsoft 資料流活動</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1288">Microsoft Stream activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1289">您可以在 Microsoft 資料流中搜尋活動的稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1289">You can search the audit log for activities in Microsoft Stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1290">這些活動包括使用者、 群組通道活動及系統管理員活動，例如管理使用者、 管理組織的設定，以及匯出報告所執行的視訊活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1290">These activities include video activities performed by users, group channel activities, and admin activities such as managing users, managing organization settings, and exporting reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1291">如需這些活動的說明，請參閱 < <b0>Microsoft Stream 中的稽核記錄</b0>的 「 登入 Microsoft Stream 的活動 」 一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1291">For a description of these activities, see the "Activities logged in Microsoft Stream" section in [Audit Logs in Microsoft Stream](https://docs.microsoft.com/stream/audit-logs).</span></span>

### <a name="exchange-admin-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1292">Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1292">Exchange admin audit log</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1293">Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄 — 這會啟用 Office 365 中的預設 — 當系統管理員身分 （或已被指派系統管理權限的使用者） 中 Exchange Online 組織進行變更時，在 Office 365 稽核記錄檔中記錄事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1293">Exchange administrator audit logging—which is enabled by default in Office 365—logs an event in the Office 365 audit log when an administrator (or a user who has been assigned administrative permissions) makes a change in your Exchange Online organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1294">使用 Exchange 系統管理中心或 Windows PowerShell 中執行指令程式來進行的變更都會記錄在 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1294">Changes made by using the Exchange admin center or by running a cmdlet in Windows PowerShell are logged in the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1295">如需詳細資訊的相關系統管理員稽核記錄功能在 Exchange，請參閱[系統管理員稽核記錄](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=619225)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1295">For more detailed information about admin audit logging in Exchange, see [Administrator audit logging](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=619225).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1296">以下是搜尋 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄中的活動的一些秘訣：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1296">Here are some tips for searching for activity in the Exchange admin audit log:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1297">若要從 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄中傳回項目，您必須在**活動**清單中選取 [**顯示所有活動的結果**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1297">To return entries from the Exchange admin audit log, you have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1298">使用日期範圍] 方塊和 [**使用者**] 清單來縮小搜尋結果在特定日期範圍內的特定 Exchange 系統管理員所執行的指令程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1298">Use the date range boxes and the **Users** list to narrow the search results for cmdlets run by a specific Exchange administrator within a specific date range.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1299">若要顯示來自 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄的事件，篩選搜尋結果，並類型**-**（虛線） 在 [**活動**篩選] 方塊中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1299">To display events from the Exchange admin audit log, filter the search results and type a **-** (dash) in the **Activity** filter box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1300">這會顯示指令程式名稱，會顯示在 Exchange 系統事件的 [**活動**] 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1300">This will display cmdlet names, which are displayed in the **Activity** column for Exchange admin events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1301">然後您可以排序依字母順序排列的指令程式名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1301">Then you can sort the cmdlet names in alphabetical order.</span></span> 
    
    ![若要篩選 Exchange 系統管理事件的活動] 方塊中輸入一條虛線](media/7628e7aa-6263-474a-a28b-2dcf5694bb27.png)
  
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1303">若要取得哪些 cmdlet 所執行、 已使用的參數和參數值，以及哪些物件受到影響的相關資訊，您必須匯出搜尋結果，並選取 [**下載所有結果**] 選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1303">To get information about what cmdlet was run, which parameters and parameter values were used, and what objects were affected, you will have to export the search results and select the **Download all results** option.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1304">您也可以使用 Exchange 系統管理中心，來檢視 Exchange 系統管理員稽核記錄中的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1304">You can also view events in the Exchange admin audit log by using the Exchange admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1305">如需相關指示，請參閱 <<c0>檢視系統管理員稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1305">For instructions, see [View the administrator audit log](https://technet.microsoft.com/library/dn342832%28v=exchg.150%29.aspx).</span></span>
  
## <a name="frequently-asked-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="279bf-1306">常見問題集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1306">Frequently asked questions</span></span>

**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1307">哪裡可以找到關於 Office 365 中的稽核服務所提供的功能？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1307">Where can I find about the features offered by the auditing service in Office 365?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1308">如需 Office 365 中可用的稽核和報告功能的詳細資訊，請參閱[稽核與 Office 365 中的報告](office-365-auditing-and-reporting-overview.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1308">For more information about the auditing and reporting features available in Office 365, see [Auditing and Reporting in Office 365](office-365-auditing-and-reporting-overview.md).</span></span> 

**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1309">什麼是目前稽核的不同 Office 365 服務？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1309">What are different Office 365 services that are currently audited?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1310">最常使用的 Office 365 服務 like Exchange Online、 SharePoint Online、 OneDrive for Business、 Azure Active Directory、 Microsoft Teams、 Dynamics 365、 進階威脅防護，和 Power BI 受到稽核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1310">The most used Office 365 services like Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, Azure Active Directory, Microsoft Teams, Dynamics 365, Advanced Threat Protection, and Power BI are audited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1311">請參閱[本文開頭](search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance.md)的稽核的服務清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1311">See the [beginning of this article](search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance.md) for a list of services that are audited.</span></span>

**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1312">查看活動稽核稽核 Office 365 中的服務？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1312">What activities are audited by auditing service in Office 365?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1313">請參閱本文章的清單和說明稽核 Office 365 中的活動的[稽核活動](#audited-activities)一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1313">See the [Audited activities](#audited-activities) section in this article for a list and description of the activities that are audited in Office 365.</span></span>

**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1314">多久需要事件發生之後才能使用稽核記錄？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1314">How long does it take for an auditing record to be available after an event has occurred?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1315">大部分的稽核資料有 30 分鐘內，但可能需要最多 24 小時之後事件發生於對應的稽核記錄項目顯示在搜尋結果中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1315">Most auditing data is available within 30 minutes but it may take up to 24 hours after an event occurs for the corresponding audit log entry to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1316">請參閱本文顯示的時間不同 Office 365 服務中的事件，可供[您開始之前](#before-you-begin)] 區段中的表格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1316">See the table in the [Before you begin](#before-you-begin) section of this article that shows the time it takes for events in the different Office 365 services to be available.</span></span>

**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1317">多久會稽核記錄保留？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1317">How long are the audit records retained for?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1318">如先前所述，稽核記錄的保留期間，取決於貴組織的 Office 365 訂用帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1318">As previously explained, the retention period for audit records depends on your organization's Office 365 subscription.</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1319">**Office 365 E3** -稽核記錄會保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1319">**Office 365 E3** - Audit records are retained for 90 days.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1320">**Office 365 E5** -稽核記錄保留為 365 天 （一年）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1320">**Office 365 E5** - Audit records are retained for 365 days (one year).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1321">適用於具有 E3 訂閱和 Office 365 進階合規性附加元件訂閱的組織，也是一年保留稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1321">Retaining audit records for one year is also available for organizations that have an E3 subscription and an Office 365 Advanced Compliance add-on subscription.</span></span>

     > [!NOTE]
     > <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1322">如同先前的說明，E5 組織 （或具有進階合規性的附加元件授權的 E3 組織） 的稽核記錄的一年保留期間是目前無法使用僅做為私人預覽計畫的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1322">As previously explained, the one-year retention period for audit records for E5 organizations (or E3 organizations that have Advanced Compliance add-on licenses) is currently available only as part of a private preview program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1323">若要在此預覽計畫中註冊，請與[Microsoft 支援服務](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/office365/admin/contact-support-for-business-products?redirectSourcePath=%252fen-us%252farticle%252fcontact-support-for-business-products-admin-help-32a17ca7-6fa0-4870-8a8d-e25ba4ccfd4b&view=o365-worldwide&tabs=online)歸檔，並包括下列項目為您需要協助的描述: 「 長期 Office 365 稽核記錄檔私人預覽 」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1323">To enroll in this preview program, please file a request with [Microsoft Support](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/office365/admin/contact-support-for-business-products?redirectSourcePath=%252fen-us%252farticle%252fcontact-support-for-business-products-admin-help-32a17ca7-6fa0-4870-8a8d-e25ba4ccfd4b&view=o365-worldwide&tabs=online) and include the following as the description of what you need help with: "Long-term Office 365 audit log private preview".</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1324">也請注意的稽核記錄的保留期間的持續時間根據每位使用者授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1324">Also note that the duration of the retention period for audit records is based on per-user licensing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1325">例如，如果您組織中的使用者指派 Office 365 版 E3 授權，該使用者所執行的活動的稽核記錄會保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1325">For example, if a user in your organization is assigned an Office 365 E3 license, then the audit records for activities performed by that user are retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1326">如果 Office 365 E5 授權指派給不同的使用者，其稽核記錄會保留一年。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1326">If a different user is assigned an Office 365 E5 license, their audit records are retained for one year.</span></span> 

**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1327">我可以透過程式設計方式存取稽核資料？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1327">Can I access the auditing data programmatically?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1328">是。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1328">Yes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1329">Office 365 管理活動 API 用來以程式設計方式擷取稽核記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1329">The Office 365 Management Activity API is used to fetch the audit logs programmatically.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1330">若要開始，請參閱 <<c0>開始使用 Office 365 管理 Api。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1330">To get started, see [Get started with Office 365 Management APIs](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/get-started-with-office-365-management-apis).</span></span>

**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1331">是否有其他方法來取得稽核記錄檔之外使用安全性與合規性中心或 Office 365 管理活動 API？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1331">Are there other ways to get auditing logs other than using the security and compliance center or the Office 365 Management Activity API?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1332">否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1332">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1333">以下是從 Office 365 稽核服務取得資料的只有兩種方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1333">These are the only two ways to get data from the Office 365 auditing service.</span></span> 

**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1334">是否需要個別啟用 [每項服務，我想要擷取稽核記錄中的稽核？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1334">Do I need to individually enable auditing in each service that I want to capture audit logs for?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1335">在大多數的 Office 365 服務中，會啟用稽核預設之後您最初開啟稽核 Office 365 組織 （如本文[開始前](#before-you-begin)一節所述）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1335">In most Office 365 services, auditing is enabled by default after you initially turn on auditing for your Office 365 organization (as described in the [Before you begin](#before-you-begin) section in this article).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1336">不過，您必須啟用稽核的每個您想要稽核的信箱在 Exchange Online 信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1336">However, you have to enable mailbox auditing in Exchange Online for each mailbox that you want to audit.</span></span>   <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1337">我們正在啟用信箱稽核根據預設會針對 Office 365 組織中所有信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1337">We are working on enabling mailbox auditing by default for all mailboxes in an Office 365 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1338">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 「 Exchange 信箱稽核會預設為啟用 「 [Microsoft 安全性、 隱私權和規範部落](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Security-Privacy-and-Compliance/Exchange-Mailbox-Auditing-will-be-enabled-by-default/ba-p/215171)格中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1338">For more information, see "Exchange mailbox auditing will be enabled by default" in the [Microsoft Security, Privacy, and Compliance blog](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Security-Privacy-and-Compliance/Exchange-Mailbox-Auditing-will-be-enabled-by-default/ba-p/215171).</span></span>

**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1339">沒有 Office 365 稽核服務支援重複資料刪除的記錄？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1339">Does the Office 365 auditing service support de-duplication of records?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1340">否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1340">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1341">稽核服務管線接近即時，，，因此無法支援重複資料刪除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1341">The auditing service pipeline is near real time, and therefore can't support de-duplication.</span></span>
 
**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1342">沒有 Office 365 稽核資料流程跨地區嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1342">Does Office 365 auditing data flow across geographies?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1343">否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1343">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1344">我們目前沒有稽核 NA （北美洲）、 （歐洲、 中東和非洲） EMEA 和 APAC （亞太地區） 區域中的管線部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1344">We currently have auditing pipeline deployments in the NA (North America), EMEA (Europe, Middle east and Africa) and APAC (Asia Pacific) regions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1345">不過，我們可能會將資料流經這些區域的負載平衡和只期間 live 網站問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1345">However, we may flow the data across these regions for load-balancing and only during live-site issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1346">當我們執行動作執行這些活動時，傳輸中的資料會加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1346">When we do perform these activities, the data in transit is encrypted.</span></span>   
 
**<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1347">稽核加密的資料嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1347">Is auditing data encrypted?</span></span>**

<span data-ttu-id="279bf-1348">稽核資料會儲存在其中部署稽核管線的相同區域中的 Exchange 信箱 （靜態資料）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1348">Auditing data is stored in Exchange mailboxes (data at rest) in the same region where the auditing pipeline is deployed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1349">此資料不會加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1349">This data is not encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="279bf-1350">不過，永遠加密傳輸中的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="279bf-1350">However, data in transit is always encrypted.</span></span>
